http://www.fast.ai/
use script and GCP SDK to create NEW GPU vm instance:

# if you want to delete existing one, firstly run commands in https://github.com/telescopeuser/fastai-setup/blob/master/bash/fastai-instance-remove.ps1

in iss-vm, open terminal:
$ gcloud init

# make sure Google Cloud Platform authentication is successful, then:

wget https://github.com/telescopeuser/fastai-setup/blob/master/bash/gcp-asia-east1.sh
bash gcp-asia-east1.sh

SSH into GCP new GPU vm instance fastai-instance:
gcloud compute --project gz-deep-learning ssh --zone asia-east1-a fastai-instance
gcloud compute ssh fastai-instance
